fix ranges\n122:  * from their location in the linted JS to the original offset in the Markdown.\n123:  * Configuration comments and indentation trimming both complicate this process.\n124:  *\n125:  * Configuration comments appear in the linted JS but not in the Markdown code\n126:  * block. Fixes to configuration comments would cause undefined behavior and\n127:  * should be ignored during postprocessing. Fixes to actual code after\n128:  * configuration comments need to be mapped back to the code block after\n129:  * removing any offset due to configuration comments.\n130:  *\n131:  * Fenced code blocks can be indented by up to three spaces at the opening\n132:  * fence. Inside of a list, for example, this indent can be in addition to the\n133:  * indent already required for list item children. Leading whitespace inside\n134:  * indented code blocks is trimmed up to the level of the opening fence and does\n135:  * not appear in the linted code. Further, lines can have less leading\n136:  * whitespace than the opening fence, so not all lines are guaranteed to have\n137:  * the same column offset as the opening fence.\n138:  *\n139:  * The source code of a non-configuration-comment line in the linted JS is a\n140:  * suffix of the corresponding line in the Markdown code block. \\treturn leadingWhitespaceRegex.exec(\\n116: \\t\\ttext.slice(getBeginningOfLineOffset(node)),\\n117: \\t)[0];\\n118: }\\n119: \\n120: /**\\n121:  * When applying fixes, the postprocess step needs to process.\\n124:  *\\n125:  * Configuration comments appear in the linted JS but not in the Markdown code\\n126:  * block. Fixes to configuration comments would cause undefined behavior and\\n127:  * should be ignored during postprocessing. Fixes to actual code after\\n128:  * configuration comments need to be mapped back to the code block after\\n129:  * removing any offset due to configuration comments.\\n130:  *\\n131:  * Fenced code blocks can be indented by up to three spaces at the opening\\n132:  * fence. Leading whitespace inside\\n134:  * indented code blocks is trimmed up to the level of the opening fence and does\\n135:  * not appear in the linted code.
